Shandong Education Expansion Plan 77

▲ Planning to add more than 100 junior high classes and more than 20 normal and commercial high school classes

▲ Adding a medical school and planning to add a junior high school

▲ Funding increased by 270,000 to 80,000 yuan compared to last year

Jinan Communication: Last year, the situation in Shandong was peaceful, education returned to normal, and schools at all levels were able to proceed according to the planned schedule. Now, at the beginning of the new year, the Department of Education is compiling an education expansion plan for the 21st year. Although it has not been completely finalized, it has been generally determined. The following is a summary: (1) Regarding senior high and normal schools, the number of junior high school graduates is increasing daily, and it is necessary to plan to add senior high classes to prepare for further education. Because senior high schools are located in Jinan, fearing that it would be inconvenient for students from other counties to study, senior high classes were specially attached to provincial middle schools in various counties last year. This year, the number of junior high school graduates in various places has increased, and it is necessary to add senior high classes to accommodate them. In the plan, the Provincial Fourth Middle School (Huimin), Fifth Middle School (Linyi), Sixth Middle School (Heze), and Eighth Middle School (Yantai) will each add two senior high classes. There are also many female middle school graduates. If it is convenient for them to study, adding a girls' senior high school would cost too much, so it was decided to add one senior class to the Jinan Provincial Girls' Middle School. It was also decided to increase the number of classes in rural normal schools. In addition to adding one class to the First Rural Normal School in Jinan, the five rural normal schools in Pingyuan, Huimin, Laiyang, Yanzhou, and Linyi will each add two classes. Post-secondary normal schools will also add classes, but the number has not yet been determined. (1) Regarding junior high schools, according to statistics from the Department of Education, more than 10,000 elementary school graduates in the province in the 20th year of the Republic of China. If half of them, 5,000, go on to further education, the existing number of junior high classes will not be able to accommodate them, and junior high classes should be expanded to meet the urgent need and avoid the congestion of last year. (Last year, all middle school entrance exams could not accommodate all applicants. Jinan No. 1 Middle School recruited 160 people, and more than 2,000 people applied.) Therefore, the Department of Education decided that in the 21st year, provincial junior high schools in the province must add at least 70 classes, and county and private junior high schools will also expand by more than 30 classes. (1) Regarding elementary schools, the Jinan Provincial First and Second Experimental Elementary Schools will increase the number of classes this year, and the Pingyuan and Huimin Rural Normal Schools will each have a central elementary school in each place (i.e., experimental elementary school). (1) Regarding the addition of new schools, it was previously passed by the provincial government meeting that in the 21st year, Shandong would establish a provincial medical school (recruiting senior high school graduates) and attach a hospital. The president has been appointed as Yin Xinong, and it is expected that the school principal will also be Yin (the hospital is separate). The funding is said to be more than 10,000 yuan per month. In addition, Shandong currently has 12 provincial middle schools, and it is planned to add another one, but the location has not yet been determined. In summary, Shandong plans to add one medical school in the 21st year (one junior high school has not been determined), add more than 100 junior high classes, eight middle school classes, 11 rural normal classes, and several post-secondary normal classes, a total of more than 20 classes. Experimental elementary schools will also add several classes. The required education funding will naturally increase. (In the 20th year, Shandong's recurring education expenses were more than 2.5 million yuan, and temporary expenses were more than 300,000 yuan, totaling more than 2.8 million yuan, so the funding for the 21st year will increase by about 270,000 to 80,000 yuan, totaling more than 3 million yuan. This budget is currently being compiled.

There is a Rumor of Changes in the Director of the Anhui Department of Education 78

▲ Han Anguang's promotion is considered promising as a successor

It has been more than a month since the central government issued a clear order appointing He Qigong as the director of the Anhui Department of Education. At first, the fellow villagers' organizations in various places outside Anhui Province strongly opposed his appointment. Then, the Anhui Education Research Association sent a telegram of opposition. He, considering the complex situation and financial difficulties in Anhui Province, has not assumed his new post for a long time. Now, the principals of secondary schools and the responsible personnel of social education institutions in Anhui Province have gathered in the capital to demand the issuance of outstanding payments from the Ministry of Finance. He feels that the situation is getting worse and has a strong intention to resign. It is heard that the central government, considering that the Anhui provincial government is about to be reorganized, will simultaneously select virtuous and capable people to avoid stagnation in education. Among the candidates for successor, the former director of the Anhui Department of Education, Han Angang, and Guang Sheng, etc., have the highest calls.

Central University Business School Retains President Zhu 80

▲ The Medical School also expressed the same sentiment

After Zhu Jiahua resigned as president of Central University, for a month, there was no one in charge of the school. Professors organized a faculty meeting to preside over everything and planned to telegraph the standards for the successor president to the government for selection. Yesterday, Xu Peikun, dean of the Business School, specially convened an emergency meeting of all faculty and staff, and it was unanimously decided to retain Zhu Jiahao to return to school to resume his post. A letter was sent to the faculty meeting to solicit opinions. The general idea of the letter is as follows: Dear Sirs, since President Zhu resigned from the school, there has been no one in charge of administration, and funding has also reached a dead end. At this critical moment of survival, there is an urgent need to act. The colleagues of this college specially held a meeting today and agreed that the standards for the successor president set by the faculty meeting are complete and perfect. If a suitable person can be found, what more can be asked for? However, a new president is not easy to produce, and the Ministry of Education is at a loss. The fire is already burning, and relief is urgently needed. Rather than looking for a new person, it is better to seek the old one again. Since President Zhu served as president, his achievements have been remarkable, and he has the ability to handle funding matters. Now that the order of the head of the department has not been accepted, this school should welcome President Zhu back to the school in the name of all professors and ask the Executive Yuan to immediately withdraw the Ministry of Education's approval of President Zhu's resignation so that the foundation of the school can be stabilized and all kinds of difficulties can be solved. Therefore, we specially raise this proposal and ask your meeting to convene an emergency meeting and proceed to stabilize the overall situation as soon as possible. We are eagerly awaiting. It is also heard that the Medical School has expressed the same sentiment.

6,000 People Praise the 3-3 Tie Between Malaya and the Interport Team 87

▲ Malaya scored three goals first 丨 Interport team came back to tie

▲ The performance was superb 丨 Unexpectedly wonderful

丨 Feng, Tu, Liang, and Li added color to Malaya 丨

Yesterday, the 6,000 spectators at the baseball field were pleasantly surprised. In the farewell performance of the Malayan Overseas Chinese Football Team, they scored three times in a row against the Shanghai Interport Team in the first 35 minutes, causing Chinese and foreign people to lose color. Afterwards, the Interport team made every effort to counterattack and also scored three goals, with the first half being 3-1 and the final score being a 3-3 draw. Such a perfect end.

丨 Malaya Lineup

Liang Shutang Yan Qisheng

Yu Zhuohua Guan Xinde

Liu Jinrong Tu Kaiyuan Li Yishen

Feng Yunyou Xie Jinfu

Huang Kehou Li Wenjie

丨 Interport Team Lineup

Kaositai Lietelei

Li Ning Mo Lai

Zhou Xianyan Zha Xu Hui Sifalun

Shiduoke Dai Linjing

Huishewo Kankehan

The Situation is Like a Terrible Storm 88

The performance of the Malayan team in the first half was superb and wonderfully original. The Interport team was almost dumbfounded, and the entire field was full of cheers. The situation was like a terrible storm, with surging tides. One wave was not flat, and another wave rose. The transitions were unpredictable, the military movements were rapid, and the eyes could not follow. The opponents were evenly matched, and it was amazing to watch. In the second half, the Interport team adopted an aggressive offensive strategy, and Malaya gradually returned to defense. Although there were also advances and retreats from time to time, it was not as dramatically changing as in the first half.

Four Generals Lived Up to Their Mission 89

The success of the Malayan team is undeniably due to the participation of the four generals of the Donghua Jinan Zhun Tu Liang Li on the front lines. Feng's composure, in cooperation with Yu, made the defensive line as strong as an iron wall. Tu's midfield, supplemented by Liang and Huang, added another solid defensive line. Huang was also satisfactory. With Li Yishen in charge of the center forward, the front line was revitalized, appearing and disappearing in the enemy's formation with great activity. The four generals of both sides also doubled their efforts, so each one was like a sea tiger, brave and invincible. Liu Jinrong's goalkeeping was also no less than Huang Jinbo's.

Five Tiger Generals Surrounded 90

The ferocity of the Interport's five tigers is undeniable, so they adopted a strict defensive policy from the beginning, with each person responsible for defending one person. Tu Kaiyuan took Hui Sifalun, the two midfielders against the two inside forwards, Liang Shutang took Dai Linjing, Huang Kehou took Mo Lai, and the two wingers were defended by Feng and Yu, one step away. The defenses were strict. Sure enough, water and fire were incompatible, so the Interport's five tigers were frustrated, discouraged and returned. The forwards were under the left and right command of Li Yishen, with triangular movements, extremely sharp.

Head-on Collision Scoring Three Goals 91

The three goals scored by Malaya first, the first to open the scoring was Li Yishen, followed by right winger Li Wenjie, and the third was left winger Yan Qisheng. The three goals were all clear, rapid and powerful shots, without any pretense, hitting the target with a crisp sound. The Interport's three goals were all due to a slight carelessness on the part of the defenders. Lietelei replaced Chen Zhenhe, which was not as good as breaking through, and Kaositai's midfielder was also mediocre.

The Momentum of the Malayan Team was Mighty 92

Malaya kicked off, against the wind and against the day's advantage. Zhaxu sent the left wing from Mo Lai to the center forward. Mo Lai raised his foot and shot, flying over the goal. Malaya began to press forward. Li Yishen passed the ball to Yan Qisheng, who flew forward. Guan Xinde pushed to the right, a very good opportunity, but Li Wenjie could not catch up, which was a pity. Mo Lai came again, and Yu Zhuohua kicked it out. Malaya issued an order for a general attack again. Xie Jinfu caught the ball and flew to Yan Qisheng. Yan shot at the goal from a distance. Zhou Xianyan caught it, but Li Yishen came again in an instant. Ning cleared it out of bounds. The corner kick was very good. Li headed it but did not score. Liang Shutang rushed over and shot from a distance, but it went out of the goal. The momentum was strong and impressive. Li Yishen's performance was especially amazing.

Li Yishen's Amazing Shot 93

Li Yishen was known to be a great general, but yesterday he suddenly showed his lifelong skills, charging left and right, commanding the advance and retreat, indescribably. Zhaxu was shocked and did not know what to do, and quickly added heavy defenses, but in the end, there was nothing he could do. Li Yishen opened the scoring with a cannon shot. The Interport besieged the goal but could not score. Kaositai fouled, and Tu Kaiyuan kicked a free kick in the middle line. Jie caught it and sent it to Li Wenjie's right corner. Although Zhou Xianyan blocked it, the right winger came again. Xie Jinfu hooked back and Li Yishen was one step faster, but one step slower, with no difference in speed, and shot into the goal, with applause like thunder, about fifteen minutes.

An Amazing Record of Three to Zero 94

Malaya's momentum did not diminish. Xie Quanfu got Li Yishen's ball. There was no one in front of the goal. It would be a pity not to shoot. Although the Interport attacked fiercely and defended strictly, it still could not score. Liang Shutang intercepted the ball and sent it forward. Yan Qisheng passed to Li Yishen. Zhou Xianyan saw that the situation was very dangerous and rushed out of the goal. Li dodged and sent it to the right. Right winger Li Wenjie flew to the shot, Malaya actually dealt with the Interport team with two to zero. In less than ten minutes, Li Wenjie passed to Li Yishen in front of the goal. The ball was too fast and Li Yishen could not attack and shoot, which was a pity. Yan Qisheng caught up and shot, it was too fast to save. Malaya actually won two games, and the whole field cheered like crazy.

Sending Two Goals in a Blur 95

Just as we were celebrating the victory, the Interport team secretly passed Chen Cang. Kankehan advanced on the right, passed from the right to the center, from the center to the right, and Mo Lai shot in the left corner, making the first half three to one. Switching goals to fight again, the Interport team kicked off. Once, Li Yishen and others advanced together. Guan Xinde did not shoot in front of the goal, so he missed the opportunity. The Interport then actively ordered a counterattack. Feng Yunyou drove east and west to rescue, and his hard work was commendable. The Interport repeatedly shot but did not score, and Malaya also got the ball and pressed forward. Shiduoke kicked it out. Huisifalun advanced on horseback, reaching the front of the goal. Yu Zhuohua wanted to let the goalkeeper kick it out, and Huishewo got to shoot, making it three to two.

A Satisfactory Ending of Three to Three 96

The Interport continued to attack non-stop. The situation was dangerous, and the entire line ordered strict defense to ensure victory. They advanced when they had the opportunity. The storms in front of the two goals were also endless, and the dangerous situation was amazing. Malaya was in a resting state due to the fierce battle in the previous game, and Li Yishen's foot was also injured. The Interport's pressure became even more intense. In the last eight minutes, Kankehan advanced directly on the right wing and passed to the front of the goal in the right corner. Dai Linjing hooked it back, and Lietelei ran over and shot it in, making it three to three, a satisfactory conclusion.

Last Week's Gold Price Trended Lower 98

▲ Changes Occurred Frequently

The gold market last week was unpredictable, with fluctuations of more than ten taels per day. The industry was indecisive. The beginning of the week was good, breaking through the 700 tael mark, but as large orders were withdrawn, it gradually weakened and fell for four consecutive days. By Friday, it suddenly dropped to 666.2 taels, which was indeed due to the unstable situation and public anger leading to market closures. The entire week saw a total decline of 34.8 taels. Near the end, there was a sign of recovery, rebounding to 680 taels, resulting in a total drop of 12.9 taels, a reaction from the four consecutive weeks of gains. On Saturday, due to the rollover, the forward rates were discounted by buyers, but the discount was limited to only 4 taels, with a maximum of 4.78 taels and a minimum of 1.78 taels. Major players like Baoyuan were willing to rollover their long positions, mainly because they had ample cash reserves and shipments from the north were arriving in Shanghai. In overseas silver markets, the trend was different: the British market contracted against the American market, and Shanghai's bill of exchange rate rose, while the domestic market tightened, which was actually affected by the surge in British and American exchange rates. The exchange rate of the US dollar, both official and unofficial, rose. Although there were no major news events abroad, there were issues like indemnity payments and proposals to raise silver prices, which were related to gold prices. Settlement prices were calculated in US dollars, ranging from 55 to 60 taels. Gold shops were actively trading in US dollars, and there were occasional squeezes. Arbitrageurs closed their positions at a profit of 30 taels. Guangbang Shen Da, etc., stepped in to close their previous short positions. The general situation of the past week is summarized below.

▲ A Drop of 12.9 Taels

On Tuesday, the large order discount reduced to 0.0625, the forward rate remained unchanged, the American silver discount was 0.25 shillings unchanged, the internal US dollar tightened slightly. The spot gold price opened at 699.5 taels, immediately rising 6.1 taels, then reaching 701 taels. Unexpectedly, sellers became active and gradually lowered the price to 98 taels at noon, and 98.5 taels in the afternoon. Guangbang sold to arbitrage bills of exchange, closing at 96.7 taels, a large increase of 3.3 taels compared to last Saturday. The 'chiseled red' (tax) was increased by 10 taels because Yufeng Yong bought in. On Tuesday, the large order discount rose again to 0.125 to 0.0625, American silver remained unchanged, the shilling was the same, the US dollar tightened slightly, while the domestic market loosened, with more sellers than buyers. Later, it was heard that Germany was buying silver and that the exchange market was loose and oversupplied, plummeting more than 8 taels and closing at 88.1 taels, a decrease of 8.6 taels compared to the previous day. The 'chiseled red' (tax) was increased by 9 taels. Securities

Only Two Days of Trading in the Bond Market Last Week 101

▲ Due to Rumors of Suspended Payments... Auctions Suspended from Wednesday

The trading situation in the Shanghai Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange market last week (from January 11th to 16th) was characterized by market instability. In reality, trading occurred only during the first two days of the week. Both spot and futures markets were quiet, with only sporadic transactions in various bonds. Major players were very cautious in their buying and selling. Total spot transactions amounted to 62,000 yuan, and futures transactions amounted to 10.07 million yuan. Transactions for the following bonds were: China Salt Tax (January term) - 1.525 million yuan, (February) - 520,000 yuan; Consolidated Tax (January) - 1.385 million yuan, (February) - 445,000 yuan; 20 Customs (January) - 1.3 million yuan, (February) - 360,000 yuan; 19 Customs (January) - 1.535 million yuan, (February) - 20,000 yuan; Nianjuan (January) - 660,000 yuan, (February) - 350,000 yuan; 19 Charity (January) - 700,000 yuan, (February) - 30,000 yuan; Disarmament (January) - 440,000 yuan, (February) - 45,000 yuan; Bianyi (January) - 410,000 yuan, (February) - 5,000 yuan; Zhengliu (January) - 155,000 yuan; Customs Tax (January) - 120,000 yuan; 96 (January) - 60,000 yuan, (February) - 5,000 yuan. Although prices remained weak on Monday, the trend was relatively peaceful, with slight increases for the 20 Customs and Salt Tax bonds of the current month. On Tuesday, market sentiment became more nervous, and the decline accelerated, with all prices falling uniformly. The trading range between the two days was approximately 2 yuan. Compared to the previous week, only the 20 Customs bond of the January term rose by 7 jiao, while most other bonds continued to fall by 1 to over 3 yuan. From Tuesday onwards, the overall situation became serious, with reports circulating from various provinces of tax revenues being withheld, and the government, facing financial difficulties, being forced to suspend payments of principal and interest on bonds. Although these rumors were unconfirmed, market sentiment became highly apprehensive. Silver and money industries and bondholders gathered to discuss countermeasures, and other industries also sent urgent telegrams requesting relief, as bond investments had truly spread across all sectors, with far-reaching connections. In light of the situation, the Exchange, for prudence's sake, announced on Wednesday morning a temporary suspension of new transactions. At the same time, brokers decided to suspend trading for two days. As the overall situation showed no improvement by Friday, it was decided to extend the suspension for another two days, awaiting news from the Ministry of Finance and whether various industries could find a solution to the problem, before deciding whether to reopen the market. Therefore, there has been no trading for four days, and the future of the bond market is not promising. Yarn and Cotton

Spot Yarn Up 1-2 Taels Last Week 102

▲ Sichuan and Guangdong Merchants Actively Stock Up

The yarn market was unusually gloomy last week, due to the increasingly severe Japanese aggression in the Northeast. The capture of Jinzhou caused discouragement, the securities market was suspended, and financing was extremely tight. As a result, the market was weak and unable to rally, with a significant risk of decline. Fortunately, there was a shortage of bottom goods in Sichuan, and purchasing in Shanghai was continuous, leading to the purchase of a considerable amount of yarn, reducing the inventory of local yarn. However, in recent times, the Japanese conducted secret operations very aggressively, with shipments from all directions. Some Japanese factories even cleared their goods at cost. The majority of spot yarn was sold off, and in light of the national crisis and tight credit, there was a unanimous trend to sell off. However, due to thin inventories and firm manufacturer sentiment, there were rumors of a squeeze on this month's contracts. According to reports, Rongxing bought over 7,000 bales, Yichang over 6,000 bales, and some sellers were manufacturers, with approximately several thousand bales scheduled for delivery. Given the situation in the business arena, a decline is unlikely in the short term, and it is difficult to predict how high the price will rise. The actions of the Sichuan and Guangdong merchants were truly significant this week, while other merchants were unremarkable. The price of spot yarn increased by 2.3 taels for this month, 1.5 taels for the middle month, and 0.8-0.9 taels for the distant months. A comparison table is as follows:

Oil Market

White Tung Oil in a Stable Process 107

For the past ten years, white tung oil has relied entirely on export sales. Since the sharp decline in overseas sales routes two years ago, the market has seen very few bright prospects. Recalling the market price three years ago, it was constantly above 30 taels, but in the past two or three years, it has been only 22-23 taels, and the total number of exports has also decreased from over 50,000 tons to 20,000 tons. For this reason, the ups and downs of the Hankou market are not as strong as before. Last year, the ups and downs did not exceed 3 taels. The decline in its momentum can be seen generally. According to recent details from Hankou, foreign firms are still purchasing, but each time it is only a few dozen tons, and the price has been fixed at slightly above 22 taels. Southern merchants have bid at 18.3-4 qian, and Sichuan tung oil is around 19 taels. The market is more than stable, but lacks sharpness, and there is no upward trend. Although local firms rely on Zhejiang and Hunan, they still rely on the Hankou market. In recent days, the Hangzhou firms have been selling special grey zhe at 30.46 yuan, but buyers are still unwilling, because the Hankou market is cheaper than before, and the Hangzhou market has not shown a drop in price. It is said that the reason why the Hangzhou market has not fallen is that the number of sales in the producing area has been high, the spot goods are very thin, and the price of seeds is difficult to drop, so the cost seems difficult to calculate. According to Jinhua, Lanhua, and other places, the cost of Xizhe boxed tung oil is 29.46 yuan, which is difficult to drop further when it arrives in Hangzhou. It is likely that it will pass the closing period in this stable state, and then the profit and loss will be determined.

Local News

Yesterday's Citizens' Assembly 109

! Temporary Martial Law in the Chinese-Administered and Mixed Settlement Areas!

▲ At the Public Sports Ground

▲ Disturbances Occurred at the Assembly

▲ One Seriously Injured and One Arrested

▲ Crowds Went to City Hall to Petition

Various people's organizations convened a citizens' assembly at the West Gate Public Sports Ground at 10:00 AM yesterday. About 2,000 people from more than 60 organizations attended. Over 30 proposals were passed on the spot. However, there was a minor dispute at the assembly, resulting in one person being injured and one arrested. After the meeting, the crowd went to the City Hall to petition for the release of the arrested compatriots, but dispersed without success. Yesterday, the areas bordering the Chinese-Administered and Mixed Settlements were under very strict guard. The details of the situation are recorded below.

Declaration of Martial Law 110

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, having received prior reports that reactionary elements had infiltrated, ordered each district, branch office, and police station to declare special martial law yesterday. Police officers were fully armed, and police brigades and mobile patrols were also conducting armed patrols. The French Concession police force declared martial law after 12:00 AM the previous night. All iron gates along the Xiejiao, Nanyangqiao, Xiaobeimen, Xiaodongmen, and Minguo Roads were tightly closed. Barbed wire fences were set up in areas bordering the Chinese-Administered areas like Lujiiawan and Dapuqiao, and large numbers of Chinese and foreign detectives were armed and stationed. The Public Settlement police force also ordered all detectives to be on full alert for maximum security.

Vehicle Service Suspended 111

The China General Omnibus Company suspended service of China General buses on route 2 (West Gate to Dongjiadu), route 3 (circular route), and route 4 (West Gate to Gaochangmiao) starting at 10:00 AM yesterday. The Shanghai South Public Bus Company suspended service of public buses on route 3 (circular route) and route 1 (West Gate to Longhua) starting at 11:00 AM yesterday. In the Public Settlement, tram routes 14, 15, 16, 17, and 19 only ran as far as Avenue Edward VII. In the French Concession, tram route 3 (Xiaodongmen to West Gate) and route 6 (Shiliupu to West Gate) were suspended, while route 5 only ran as far as Avenue d'Orleans. Service for China General Buses and Public Buses was restored starting at 3:00 PM.

Crowd at the Citizens' Assembly (Photo by this newspaper)

Assembly Arrangement 112

The words "Shanghai Citizens' Assembly" were written on a banner above the entrance. Inside, a signing table was set up for attendees to sign in. A high platform was set up in the center of the assembly, with the same words as the banner written on it. The order of the assembly was posted next to it. A press table was placed in front of the platform. Personnel from various organizations stood in the middle of the assembly, with hardly any space to move.

Security at the Assembly 113

Over 30 police officers from the 3rd District were stationed at the entrance of the assembly, and mobile police patrols patrolled back and forth. The Garrison Command also sent soldiers to various locations as sentries. Detectives from the Municipal Detective Brigade were fully mobilized. Inside the assembly, a security team organized by workers from the Xihe Yarn Factory maintained order.

Attending Organizations 114

The participants in the Citizens' Assembly included over two hundred organizations, amounting to more than five thousand people, including the Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association, the Bookbinding Workers' Union, the Shenxin No. 7 Factory Workers' Anti-Japanese Association, the Tongxing Yarn Factory Workers' Union, the Telephone Company Workers' Union, the Garment Industry Union, the Dongjiadu Ferry Workers' Union, Xihe Yarn Factory Workers, the Cloth Industry Union, the West District Yarn Factory Workers' Union, the Nihua Yarn Factory Workers, the Noodle Industry Workers' Anti-Japanese Association, Modern Middle School, Vincent's English College, Shanghai University, China Physical Education College, Cultural Institute Volunteer Army, Zhizhi University, China Public School, Jiaotong University, Jinan University, Shenchang Factory, French Concession Tram Workers' Anti-Japanese Association, Chinese Students Returning from Japan Association, Pudong Middle School, the Joint Association of Anti-Japanese Associations of Various Middle Schools, etc.

Discord Occurs 115

According to the New Voice Society, around 10 AM yesterday, the Shanghai Special City Workers' Movement Committee sent people carrying a large number of leaflets. Because some of the leaflets contained phrases such as "Eradicate the Chinese Communist Party" and "Down with the Communist Party," someone beat the leaflet distributors, causing temporary chaos. At the same time, a large number of leaflets were burned with fire next to the speaker's platform on the east side. The leaflet distributing workers were beaten and injured. A police officer from the Second District Police Station sent one of the seriously injured to the hospital by car. The other one returned home to treat himself. At that time, a police officer at the gate arrested one student who was carrying reactionary leaflets and detained him to be investigated by the Municipal Public Security Bureau. (According to a survey by the Daily News Agency, the injured person's name is Liu Shaoyan, and the detained person's name is Wang Hanqing.)

Conference Staff 116

The following were publicly elected: Yuan Yiqun from the Jiaotong University Anti-Japanese Association, Lai Yixue from the Central Public Anti-Japanese Association, Wang Zhong from the People's Anti-Japanese United Association, Han Guanglin from the Xihua Yarn Factory Strike Committee, Yuan Zhenbang from the Shenxin Seventh Factory, and Cai Ruoshan from the Joint Anti-Japanese Association of Various Middle Schools as general commanders of the presidium; Ye Yulang from Jinan University as deputy commander; and Yang Zhiyuan from Jinan University as deputy commander. Liu Binghua from Jinan University was appointed as chief disciplinarian.

Chairman's Report 117

At 10:30 AM, the meeting was announced to be opened. Yuan Yiqun, the chairman of the presidium from Jiaotong University, gave a brief report, saying, "Today's citizens' assembly is based on the purpose determined by the joint meeting of various anti-Japanese organizations on the 14th of this month. Because after the violent Japanese forces forcibly occupied our three northeastern provinces, they continued to attack China relentlessly, resulting in the fall of Jinzhou and the crisis in Shanhaiguan. The government has not come up with any solutions so far. If we want to save the current crisis, we must rely on the power of the people. Compatriots, let us unite and arm ourselves to declare war on Japanese imperialism. Therefore, please express your opinions as much as possible so as to determine concrete policies and seek the survival of the Chinese nation."

Key Resolutions 118

The main items resolved by the general meeting are as follows: ㈠ Oppose the government's selling of the three northeastern provinces and do not recognize any secret treaties or agreements; ㈡ Oppose the government's suppression of the people's movement and the massacre of anti-Japanese people; ㈢ Auction off confiscated Japanese goods to relieve striking workers and unemployed workers; ㈣ Use the power of the people to take over the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association; ㈤ All sectors organize genuine volunteer armies to declare war on Japan; ㈥ The people themselves organize Japanese goods inspection teams; ㈦ Execute the members of the Fujian Provincial Government; ㈧ The people arm themselves to prevent the partition of China and the League of Nations investigation team from coming to China; ㈨ Assist striking workers in various factories; ㈩ Oppose the government's suspension of payment of principal and interest on public bonds, indiscriminate issuance of public bonds, and secret diplomacy; ㈩㈠ Demand that the municipal government release the students and people arrested for participating in the anti-Japanese movement; ㈩㈡ Oppose the government's promulgation of the 26 articles of the Seafarers' Regulations, and other fourteen motions. In addition, the people temporarily proposed motions such as requesting the Citizens' Assembly to organize a Yong'an Factory Massacre Committee and requesting the Citizens' Assembly to sell the sealed Japanese goods at low prices to raise donations to help the workers.

Parade in Formation 119

After the adjournment of the meeting, it was already 12 o'clock. The masses who attended the meeting immediately organized themselves and set off for a parade, walking along Fangxie Road and Xietu Road, heading straight to the reactionary elements of the Municipal Government. Along the way, they sang The Internationale and shouted reactionary slogans. After reaching Fenglin Bridge, they first smashed the sign and police post in front of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. By this time, the municipal government had already closed the main gate tightly, and the Songhu Garrison Command sent a team to defend inside. Unable to enter, the masses gathered in the open space in front of the municipal government. At this time, the municipal government had already dispatched more than 60 Mauser squads and patrol cars from the Public Security Bureau, and the Garrison Command also added a platoon of infantry to guard the open space tightly.

Business Suspended 120

More than 100 stores in the Ximen Fangxie Road area, including Wannian Jewelry Store, Yuchang Store, Wanzuo Qiaji Brothers Store, Yifeng Hotel, Hengkang Xingji, Southern Company, Chunhe Foil Shop, Nantongtai, Mingxing Socks Factory, Li Bingji, and Rongchangxiang Coal Store, fearing that rioters would infiltrate and cause trouble during the citizens' assembly parade, closed their doors one after another starting at 12 o'clock yesterday morning and temporarily suspended business. It was not until 5 o'clock in the afternoon that they fully resumed operations.

(Photo by this newspaper) The speaker at the meeting

Demand Release 121

Because the Municipal Government's defense was tight, the masses who were parading in formation could not enter. They immediately sent 22 representatives to request a meeting with Mayor Wu to petition for the release of the masses arrested today. However, it happened to be Sunday, and no one in the Municipal Government was responsible for answering. Unable to get any results, it was already 4 o'clock. The entire crowd immediately convened a general meeting in the open space. The Anti-Japanese Associations of Jinan and Guanghua Universities were responsible for organizing a support association for the arrested comrades and decided to hold the first meeting at 24 Wuding Road at 6 PM today to discuss ways to rescue the arrested. After the meeting, they shouted various reactionary slogans again and continued to parade in formation.

Result of the Parade 122

The masses left the Municipal Government at 4:20 and continued to parade and demonstrate along the same route. They originally intended to return to the Public Sports Ground to gather and disband, but because the gate of the Public Sports Ground was tightly closed and they could not enter, the mood of the masses became even more tense. They then all went to the Municipal Party Headquarters. Because it was a weekend, there was not a single person in the Party Headquarters, and the gate guard had also been withdrawn. The masses completely smashed the police post and glass windows at the entrance and broke several pieces of glass upstairs with stones. Until 4:30, about 200 people formed a team and walked along Minguo Road and turned into Nanyang Bridge, throwing away the red flag. When passing through Ximen, Shanghai public buses, seeing the masses coming again, stopped all the public buses on Penglai Road until 5 o'clock before resuming operation. The masses then returned to the French Concession from Nanyang Bridge, but only about 100 people passed through the Great World and walked along Hubei Road until North Zhejiang Road, where they completely dispersed.

Worker Donations 123

Before the meeting, more than 30 female workers from the striking Xihua and other Japanese-owned yarn factories formed a fundraising team. Wearing white cloth on their chests and carrying bamboo tubes, they went to the Laoximen area to raise donations from shops and pedestrians. The response to donations was quite enthusiastic.

Please also ask Brother Hanliang to come to Beijing tonight to discuss various matters. Sincerely, Sun Ke."

A Record of the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association's General Meeting Yesterday 126

The meeting adjourned at 7 o'clock.

▲ Appendix: Letter to the Elders, Brothers and Sisters of the Whole Country. Let the elders, brothers and sisters of the whole country know: For five years, the one-party dictatorship has been abusing people's wealth, reaching more than 200 million yuan. Talking about construction every day, even the waters of the rivers and seas have not been properly prevented and repaired, resulting in floods that have spread to 20 provinces, including Hubei, Anhui, Hunan, Henan, Jiangsu, Jiangxi, Guangdong, Zhejiang, Fujian, Shandong, Hebei, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Sichuan, Guangxi, Guizhou, Yunnan, Liaoning, Jilin and Heilongjiang. The people have suffered disasters one after another, but there has never been a plan for thorough disaster relief. More than 2 million redundant soldiers have been raised, engaging in internal strife every day, and even the border defenses of the Northeast have not been consolidated, resulting in tens of millions of military equipment being entrusted to the enemy. Watching helplessly as the three provinces are reduced to iron hooves, daring not to add a single bullet to the Japanese soldiers, enduring the lonely army of Ma Zhanshan's bitter battles, and being forced to retreat without weapons or pay, but there has never been a plan for the entire resistance against the invaders. Recently, the central government has been reorganized, and the public believes that the party members may have a heart of repentance. However, it has been delayed again and again, waiting for one of the three standing committee members to come to the capital, but it is impossible. The suicidal policy of using public debt funds suddenly rings in the ears. Is this what is meant by political tutelage? Anyone with a little knowledge and a little blood will not accept this tutelage. Our people are regretting that they trusted the party too deeply in the past. Without representatives, how can taxes be paid? They also feel that there is no hope for the party in the future and they will become slaves of a subjugated country. How can they not ask about politics? From now on, the way for our people to strive for self-salvation is to raise brave soldiers for private fights and be timid for public battles. It is better for each of them to do their best to defend their local areas. Instead of paying taxes with obligations but without rights, it is better to exercise their right to supervise the government. It is deeply hoped that the financial circles of the whole country will awaken themselves quickly. If the government has the slightest behavior that disregards credit, it must not be easily subsidized, so as to avoid the danger of financial ruin. It is especially hoped that the taxpayers of the whole country will awaken themselves quickly. If there is the slightest expenditure that cannot be made public in the locality, it must not be easily recognized, so as to build a self-governing society on the spirit of every individual being responsible. As for the failure of diplomacy, it is entirely due to the chaos of internal affairs. If those who preside over internal affairs can truly consolidate the hearts of the people, then those who handle diplomacy will naturally be able to negotiate internationally. Our people repent of their conscience and have no choice but to promote the reflection of the Japanese warlords by not using Japanese goods. They should also encourage each other as fathers and brothers and persevere without slackening. Moreover, they should cry bitterly for the Japanese goods merchants and tell them to transfer their capital for selling Japanese goods to the cause of manufacturing domestic goods. In one shift, they can achieve both fame and fortune, and their bodies and minds can be complete. What is there to enjoy and not do to change the country's aspirations? The police issued a small notice, hoping that our people will rise up together to plan it. Jiangsu Provincial National Crisis Relief Association.

Municipal Party Department Urges Hu Hanmin to Go to Beijing 128

The Shanghai Special City Party Department, due to the urgency of the national crisis and the lack of responsible persons in the central government, telegraphed Wang Jingwei, Hu Hanmin, and Chiang Kai-shek, urging them to go to Beijing to preside over the national salvation plan. Here is the text of the telegram to Hu Hanmin: "Mr. Hu Zhantang, Hong Kong, Greetings. Jinzhou has fallen, and Rehe and Hebei are shaken. The gentlemen of the new government, although they seem to have come with a plan and are fearless, have been in office for more than ten days and have not been able to come up with any solutions. Faced with this critical situation, only appealing like Qin Ting and weeping like prisoners of Chu can make up for the national affairs and help the reputation of the Party. Sir, you and Mr. Wang and Chiang have received the heavy trust of the Party and the country. You should be wary of the falling of the roof and the breaking of the rafters. Why do you cherish your feathers and refuse to come out, causing the criticism of the court and the public to be intertwined, and the Party affairs and national affairs to be more complicated? The Association, looking at the current situation, is filled with deep anxiety. In addition to telegraphing Mr. Wang and Chiang, urging them with great righteousness to go to Beijing to take responsibility, it also offers two sincere words to you, a general figure who is planning for the center of the situation and the key to governance. First, our Party is a group with a revolutionary history. In the past, under the leadership of the Premier, we risked danger and fought against the Qing government, imperialism, bureaucratic officials, and feudal forces. Anyone who benefited the country and the nation did not hesitate to risk their own lives to achieve it, so that we could gain a position in history and be loved by the majority of the people. After the death of the Premier, this heavy responsibility of leading the revolution has been placed on the shoulders of a few leaders of our Party by the Premier. Sir, you are a senior member of the comrades who have devoted themselves to the revolution, so you have a special responsibility to shoulder the arduous task. However, have you and others thought that you have fulfilled your responsibility of shouldering the arduous task? Can you still not hesitate to risk your own lives to seek the welfare of the Party, the country, and the nation? Taking our Party as an example, in the peaceful autumn in the country, there were still countless people who slandered our Party, saying that our Party's doctrine was ideal, and that our Party's political tutelage was a monopoly. Now that foreign aggression is imminent and the country is in danger of being destroyed, a few leaders of our Party who bear extraordinary responsibility, if they still deceive each other, fight each other, and do not think about uniting and facing the national crisis together, then the so-called ideal doctrine will become a deceptive fantasy, and the so-called monopoly of political tutelage will also become a situation of monopolizing but not doing anything. When the day comes when the Party is not like a Party and the country is not like a country, how can those like you escape the public criticism and the historical evaluation? This is the first reason why you, sir, should go to Beijing to take responsibility in terms of responsibility. Second, at the beginning of the Northeast Incident, the central government immediately asked you, sir, to take on the arduous task, and invited all the comrades to go to Beijing to discuss national affairs. Mr. Chiang also repeatedly stated that he was unwilling to abandon his responsibility during the national crisis and resign lightly. However, some comrades who were closely related to you in Guangzhou could not bear to serve the country and insisted on the proposal to resign. After Mr. Chiang repeatedly stated that he would never be greedy for power, Guangzhou then sent representatives to Shanghai to negotiate peace. It was heard that on the day the representatives arrived in Shanghai, you, sir, secretly instructed your relations to use the strategy of overthrowing the new warlords with Mr. Wang, and your subordinates used all kinds of methods to force Chiang to step down. In order to establish a new government and obtain your cooperation, Mr. Chiang immediately telegraphed his resignation, meaning that after stepping down, you and others would definitely put the national affairs first and immediately go to Beijing. Therefore, in keeping with his lifelong spirit of daring to take responsibility, he stayed in Beijing waiting for the car to arrive, but he did not want you and your subordinates to still be in Guangzhou, Hong Kong, Beijing, and other places, shouting loudly, that he would never come to Beijing until he left Beijing. As a result, Mr. Chiang, in order to ensure the initial intention of uniting and resisting the invaders, did not want to obstruct the progress of uniting and resisting the invaders for his own sake, so he had no choice but to leave Beijing and return to his hometown after his resignation. Now that Mr. Chiang has been out of office for a month, what other reasons do you have for not going to Beijing to take responsibility? Mr. Chiang, although he has his shortcomings in his life, also has his strengths, and he is willing to take responsibility, which is his strength. You, sir, used your own personal resentment, not wanting him to take responsibility and forcing him to resign and leave Beijing. After Chiang resigned and left Beijing, you pushed back three or four times and refused to come to Beijing to take responsibility, causing the foreign aggression to become more urgent and the national affairs to become more wrong. I don't know what your intentions are. "If you are not good, overthrow you and let me do it well." This is the behavior of a man. "If you are not good, overthrow you and let me do it," this is still not the behavior of a great man. Otherwise, using the national affairs to sacrifice one's own personal resentment and not willing to do a little duty for the Party and the country, is this what a great man would do? This is the second reason why you, sir, should go to Beijing to take responsibility in terms of morality. The comrades have no grievances against you, sir, and no virtue to Mr. Chiang. As members of the Party, we put the Party and the country first, and we dare not fail to report what we think is dangerous. If you, sir, adopt our humble opinions and go to Beijing to meet the national crisis together, then we will be very fortunate. Telegram hurriedly, with extreme trepidation. Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

Retired military officer Feng Ganchen telegraphed the Central Party Department, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that they do their best to resist the invaders and not be subdued by the violent Japanese forces. I am writing this special reply, hoping that you will check it. Chen Youren."

Record of the National Lawyers Association Meeting 131

▲ Discussion of Various Meeting Procedures

▲ Continued Meeting Today

The National Lawyers Association held an interim executive committee and representatives of various lawyers associations meeting yesterday (Sunday) at the Shanghai Lawyers Association, located at the intersection of Beiler Road and Lafayette Road in the French Concession. Those present were Liu Zu, Wang Li Shi, Liu Liumin (Executive Committee members), Hu Zhen (Executive Committee member and Zhenjiang Association representative), Luo Zhizhu, Wang Rongzhi, Liu Shixiong (Executive Committee members), Ge Xiujian (Executive Committee member and Hankou Association representative), Huang Yongchang (Executive Committee member and Yin County Association representative), Guo Wei, Zhao Chen, Shen Junru (Shanghai Association representatives), Wang Shengwu (Executive Committee member), Dai Tianqiu (Jiangdu Association representative), Fei Tinghuang, Zhang Shixuan (Wu County Association representatives), Dong Naitong, Zhang Tao (Hang County Association representatives), Tong Baoheng (Yin County Association representative), He Jianzhang (Hang County Association representative), Ye Jisheng (Guangzhou Association representative), Shan Yuhua (Executive Committee member), and Tan Yigong (Executive Committee member), totaling 23 people. Liu Liumin was publicly elected as chairman, and Dai Jiyuan was the recorder. After the ceremonial proceedings, the meeting was called to order at 3 PM after the ringing of the bell. The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, saying that today's meeting was held at the Shanghai Lawyers Association. It was a great pleasure that representatives from various associations had come from afar to gather together. The chairman reported on the purpose of today's meeting as follows: ㈠ This association should urge the judicial authorities to quickly convene a national judicial conference and establish a permanent judicial conference mechanism; ㈡ How should this association make suggestions on the revision of the criminal law and criminal procedure code? What guidance should be given to other people's organizations? Can this association monitor the members of the two houses and the national salvation conference from the standpoint of people's organizations? How should its election law be formulated? Next, representatives such as Duo Shi, Ye Xiasheng, and Liu Zuwang successively expressed their opinions and made detailed discussions. After 6 o'clock, the following methods were discussed: ㈠ The government should be requested to quickly convene a national judicial conference; ㈡ The government should be requested to establish a permanent judicial conference mechanism from now on; ㈢ The organizational members of the judicial conference are divided into (A) court representatives, (B) lawyers association representatives, and (C) representatives of professors from various law schools; ㈣ The issue of proposing the revision of the criminal procedure code was researched, and it was decided to organize a special committee for the revision of the criminal law and criminal procedure code. Shan Yuhua, Shen Junru, Zhao Chen, Guo Wei, Dai Tian Qiu, Zhang Shixuan, Lu Hongyi, He Sheidao, Zhang Tao, Dong Kang, Zhang Yaozeng, Xu Yuangao, Li Shirui, Huang Naitong, He Jianzhang, Liu Zuwang, Hu Zhen, Pan Ya, Ye Xia Sheng, Liu Liumin, Zhu Hongda, Fei Tinghuang, and Dong Rongchang were appointed as members on the spot; ㈤ The committee elected member Li Shirui as the convener; ㈥ The deadline is three weeks (starting from the date of publication in the newspaper) to complete the revision of the criminal law and criminal procedure code, on the one hand, requesting the Legislative Yuan to extend the deadline by one month, and on the other hand, notifying the various lawyers associations to contribute their opinions within February 10. Because it was already late, it was decided to continue the meeting tomorrow (that is, this morning) and adjourned.

Three Demands Telegram from the 26th Branch of the City Federation 133

The 26th branch of the City Federation sent a "Three Demands" telegram yesterday, which reads:

(1) Telegram to the National Government: The national crisis is imminent, and the destruction of the nation is close at hand. The only one who can resist the brutal Japanese is General of the Black Province who firmly defends the border. No one else has been heard of. Fortunately, the Volunteer Army, which has risen up spontaneously, is resisting the Japanese army, but it lacks support and is difficult to sustain. The Association, aware that the demise of the country is imminent, requests the government to quickly decide on a national salvation plan: A. Immediately sever relations with Japan; B. Order Zhang Xueliang, the general who lost territory, to recover the lost land. If he continues to wait and see, he should be punished by national law to appease public anger. C. Rapidly mobilize and concentrate elite forces to prepare for national defense. D. Provide the Volunteer Army with guns and ammunition and encourage them to advance together to resist Japan. E. Implement revolutionary diplomacy and request all countries to respect the treaties and refute Japan's note on the open-door policy in Manchuria. The above points are urgent tasks for national salvation. We hope that the government will make a decisive decision and implement them without delay. We look forward to it anxiously.

(2) Telegram to the US Government: Your country is a civilized nation in the world, and diplomatic relations have always been cordial. You especially advocate world peace and have seen the notes in which China and Japan fulfill the treaties. We admire your fair and just position. The so-called justice will not perish, and the world still has hope. We hope that you will uphold justice and enforce the ironclad evidence of the treaties, and strictly refute Japan's unreasonable reply note, which claims to reaffirm the open-door policy in Manchuria, which is completely sophistry. The people of our country are filled with righteous indignation, and the seizure of our country's land is said to be legal, which is even more absurd. Its actions to destroy peace in East Asia violate the Kellogg-Briand Pact. We request your country to join the signatory countries and make a final fair claim to sanction the brutal Japan and strive for world peace. We earnestly pray.

(3) Telegram to the Jinzhou Volunteer Army: Your loyalty and courage to save the country are admired by the world. The righteous banner of your army stands tall. You do not hesitate to sacrifice your life for righteousness and serve the country. You embrace the responsibility of defending the country and uphold the spirit of fearlessness from beginning to end. This enhances the glory of our nation. We rely on your army to continue to strive to annihilate the brutal enemy, remove the obstacles to world peace, and fight for the happiness of national survival. This Association pledges to be your backing.

Continued Receipt of Telegrams from the City Chamber of Commerce Opposing the Suspension of Payment of Principal and Interest on Public Bonds 134

The City Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, and other organizations in this city received two telegrams from Tianjin yesterday opposing the suspension of payment of principal and interest on public bonds. The original text is recorded as follows:

(1) To the City Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, and the Money Trade Association: It is noted that the government has news of suspending the payment of principal and interest on domestic debt. If true, it will plunge the national finance into bankruptcy and the livelihood of the entire people into desperation. The foundation of the country is at stake. How can we allow it to be shaken even slightly? In addition to separately writing to the Ministry of Finance and the Domestic Debt Fund Custody Committee to strongly argue against it, this Association pledges to follow you all as a backing. Tianjin City Chamber of Commerce, bowed and filed.

(2) To the City Chamber of Commerce, the Domestic Debt Fund Custody Committee, the Bankers' Association, and the Money Trade Association: It is noted that there is a proposal to suspend the payment of principal and interest on domestic debt. If this measure is true, the damage will be so great as to plunge the livelihood of the entire people into desperation. Fortunately, your Association has protested first. This Association is willing to cooperate and unite to be a backing. Respectfully telegraphed to you for your information. Tianjin Money Trade Association, bowed and filed, deleted.

National Association for Local Autonomy 135

▲Scheduled to convene the third annual conference

The National Association for the Advancement of Local Autonomy is a formal organization established by representatives elected by local autonomy advancement associations of various provinces, circuits, counties, and cities, in accordance with the law, to assist the government in carrying out local autonomy. Since the first conference was held in Nanjing and the second conference was held in Hangzhou, it happened to be the time of the rise of the revolutionary army. The people of the whole country are devoted to eliminating warlords and hoping to build the foundation of democratic politics, so the association affairs were temporarily suspended. Recently, the president of the association, Chu Huiseng, the general affairs minister, Wu Xiaohou, the Shanghai-based director, Shen Tianxin, the Jiangsu provincial association president, Pang Tiejie, and other important figures gathered in Shanghai to discuss. They all agreed that since the sixteenth year, internal chaos has continued, and there is still no sign of democratic politics. In addition, the banditry is becoming increasingly urgent, and foreign insults are coming one after another. The people are suffering even more than in the past. If we want to extend civil rights and seek self-salvation, there is no other way but to implement local autonomy. After separately soliciting the opinions of important figures from various temples, they all believe that the association has an unshirkable responsibility to promote local autonomy. It was decided to continue the development of local autonomy throughout the country with the spirit of the past, and to convene the third conference in Shanghai on February 21, and to temporarily set up an office at No. 13, Lianzhu Lane, Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai. In addition to publishing notices of the convening in major newspapers in Shanghai, Tianjin, Wuhan, and other four cities, separate letters were sent to local autonomy advancement associations in various places, inviting them to send representatives to attend the conference. Local autonomy enthusiasts from all over are also welcome to actively join the association so that they can gather ideas and work together to promote progress.

The Flourishing Business of the Zhabei National Products Exhibition 136

▲Reaching 40,000 Yuan per day

▲Extending business hours

The third National Products Exhibition in Zhabei, organized by the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products, officially opened on the sixteenth day after the opening was announced on the fifteenth day. The business is quite prosperous. The details are recorded as follows:

▲Exhibition Hall Arrangement: The exhibition hall is located on the square in front of the Zhabei Chamber of Commerce. It is built with Western-style bungalows, divided into eighty-four booths. Silk fabrics, cotton cloth, knitwear, woolen fabrics, and cotton fabrics each occupy four booths. Woolen cloth, copperware, combs, woolen hats, electrical appliances, and leather goods each occupy two booths. Food, glassware, jewelry, MSG, tea, enamelware, steel beds, paintbrushes, toothbrushes, paint, candles, soap, oil lamps, and toys each occupy one booth. The layout is elegant, economical, and beautiful.

▲Authorities Maintain Order: The Fourth District Office of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the Zhabei Security Regiment, and the Detective Team dispatched a large number of police officers to maintain order at the exhibition hall. A fire brigade of the Zhabei Fire Brigade carried a fire engine and four fire extinguishers to station at the exhibition hall for fire prevention. The authorities' maintenance of national products can be described as extremely complete.

▲Prosperous Business: The staff of the association are energetic and treat guests with humility and kindness, so guests feel at home. On the first day after the opening (the sixteenth day), the total business revenue of the entire exhibition hall reached more than 38,640 yuan. Among them, cotton textiles and winter supplies sold best, and the business of Wei Shunji Toy Factory was also very prosperous. According to Chen Binghui, the standing committee member of the exhibition hall, this achievement is rare in the history of exhibitions and is enough to show the citizens' growing enthusiasm for promoting national products.

▲Extending Business Hours: The original business hours of the association were from 9:00 am to 7:00 pm. However, the majority of residents and workers in Zhabei are workers from nearby factories who do not have time to go to the exhibition hall to shop after work in the evening. They have requested to extend the business hours. The association, in response to their request, has changed the daily business hours from 10:00 am to 8:30 pm starting today (the eighteenth day).

▲Publishing a Declaration: In order to awaken the citizens to promote national products consistently, the propaganda department of the association, in addition to hanging bamboo cloth slogans on the main roads of the Chinese Concession, also published a declaration and distributed it to guests from all walks of life to spread the word.

▲Responsible for handling matters related to boycotting goods

▲Establishing inspection teams to implement inspections

Seventeen trade associations in this city, including the brick and tile industry, seafood and groceries industry, seafood store industry, sugar industry, local products industry, electrical appliance industry, southern goods industry, jute bag industry, yarn industry, fly ash industry, northern and southern goods exchange industry, cotton cloth industry, silk fabric industry, new drug industry, color printing industry, sausage industry, and ginseng and velvet industry, jointly sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce, stating: We believe that the boycott of Japanese goods is closely related to commercial tools and should be carried out automatically and strictly by our merchants and people in order to achieve a thorough solution. Demands of the Staff of the Anti-Japanese Association Regarding the Layoff Case 138

Please Publicize the Accounts of the Executive Committee

▲Revoke the proposal to lay off and dismiss personnel

▲After the formal establishment of the Staff Union of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in this city, it held its first meeting the day before yesterday and specially submitted a document to the executive committee of the association yesterday regarding the layoff issue. The document stated: We respectfully submit this document for consideration. Since your association announced the resolution to lay off staff, comrades from various departments have sent representatives to your association to inquire about the reason for the layoffs. Later, Wang Xiaoyan and other committee members invited the representatives to a banquet at Hangzhou Restaurant and instructed them that the motivation for the layoffs was due to a lack of funds and promised to propose appropriate solutions to your association. After hearing this news, comrades from various departments continued to work as usual and awaited the decision of your association. Unexpectedly, at the meeting of the Native Place Association on the eleventh, Wu Mai publicly insulted our staff from various departments and proposed to dismiss all of them and have staff from various departments be filled by the relevant trade associations. The news spread and was extremely shocking. Our comrades from various departments came for the sake of patriotism, but now they have been insulted, which is not in accordance with the law or reason. Moreover, the proposals to dismiss staff and have them filled by trade associations are both contrary to the original intention of patriotism. Therefore, comrades from various departments of this association convened a plenary meeting yesterday and unanimously stated that your association suddenly decided to lay off staff and then proposed to dismiss them and have them filled by trade associations. The reasons for this are nothing more than a lack of funds and a reduction in workload. However, it is rumored that the fine money decided by your association is more than 200,000, but only 70,000 to 80,000 have been received. Now, instead of collecting the fine money, you are laying off staff due to a lack of funds. We really don't know what your association is thinking. (Omitted) Furthermore, the proposal to have staff from various departments of this association be filled by trade associations is absurd and unreasonable. The Anti-Japanese Association is organized by all the citizens, how can it be monopolized by biased elements? Although there are indeed trade associations that can fully assist this association in its anti-Japanese work, there are also many who protect unscrupulous merchants and use deceptive words. If it is once taken over by such people, the future of anti-Japanese resistance is unimaginable. If your association has such a resolution, please revoke it, otherwise it may cause a backlash from all the citizens and cause great anxiety. Comrades from various departments have summarized the reasons and decided on the following conclusions: (1) Request your association to publicize the accounts to clarify whether there is a lack of funds. (2) Request the committee members to attend the association daily to expedite the handling of matters. (3) Request the committee members to solemnly sign and approve documents to convince the public, so that the staff can work diligently. (4) Re-establish the rules for rewarding secret reports to maintain credibility. (5) When staff are oppressed outside, your association should provide full assistance to encourage them. (6) Revoke the resolutions to dismiss staff and have staff from various departments be filled by trade associations. We hope that the above points will be answered within three days to reassure the public and avoid disputes. This would be a great favor.

Workers of the Xihe Yarn Factory Decided to Propose Conditions for Resolution 144

After the strike by all Chinese workers in the first, second, and third factories of the Japanese Xihe Textile Factory in Huxi, the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau tried to mediate and the entire workers held a meeting at the Huxi Commune yesterday. The following requirements were agreed to be put forward. 1) Oppose the dismissal of workers without reason. 2) All dismissed workers must be reinstated. 3) Oppose wage cuts. 4) Oppose cancellation of monthly bonuses. 5) Oppose capitalists closing factories. 6) Wages will be paid as usual during the strike period. 7) Double salary will be given at the end of the year. 8) Workers have the freedom to organize workers. 9) Recognize the strike committee. 10) Oppose capitalists oppressing workers. 11) Female workers will be given four months of leave before and after childbirth, and a subsidy of 40 yuan for childbirth expenses. 12) Prohibit beating and scolding female workers. 13) Oppose extending working hours on Sundays. 14) Those who undermine the strike are counter-revolutionaries.

Ministry of Finance's Reply to the Request of the Property Management Office to Exempt Additional Grain Tax 146

▲Initially, the extension was not approved

▲Later, it was said that it could be done

The Shanghai County Property Management Office requested that the additional winter grain tax be exempted, and the request was submitted to the Ministry of Finance of the National Government to quickly cancel the additional two yuan to alleviate the people's difficulties. The news has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, a directive from the Ministry of Finance was received, stating that after reviewing the case file, the request to exempt the additional two yuan of grain tax has been noted. The case of Jiangsu extending the additional grain tax for one year was approved by the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan in April of the 20th year, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government was instructed to submit the proposal to extend the additional two yuan of grain tax from the 19th year for one year in the budget plan for the 20th year. The Ministry has listed the reasons why the extension could not be approved and requested to maintain the original proposal. Later, a letter from the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan was approved and sent to the Jiangsu Provincial Government to continue to submit the proposal to extend the additional two yuan of grain tax for one year. Since this case has been submitted by the Jiangsu Provincial Government together, and it is now during the period of bandit suppression, it seems that it can still be handled. However, the land tax in Jiangsu Province has always been heavy. In addition to the regular tax, there are additional taxes. During this one-year extension period, the counties must not add any additional taxes under the male tax item. After the expiration, the provincial government must not request to extend it again under any name, so that the provincial treasury and the people's difficulties can be taken care of on both sides. The letter was replied and forwarded. Subsequently, an order from the Executive Yuan was issued and the National Government was ordered to approve the record. The Ministry then ordered the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to comply with the case. You should be informed that the county has submitted the number of scores determined by the autumn survey in the 20th year, and you should also wait for the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to verify it.

Danish Company to Operate Five Giant Ships Between New York and the Far East 154

▲ New ships to launch in May

The Shanghai Times reports that the Danish Maersk Line, one of the world's most famous shipping companies, with 43 ships and routes spanning the seven seas, is managed in this city by East Asiatic Company. Since the opening of the Far East-North America route in March of last year, business has been excellent. Several weeks ago, the company's owner, Mr. Møller, visited Shanghai for inspection and decided to add five newly built oil-burning giant ships to the Pacific route. The new ships will launch by the end of May, with one sailing each month thereafter, traveling between New York and the Far East. The ships will stop at New York, Hampton Roads, Savannah, the Panama Canal, San Pedro, Yokohama, Kobe, Shanghai, Qingdao, Manila, Iloilo, and Makassar. The new ships have a speed of 15 miles per hour, requiring only 21 days from the Far East to Los Angeles, and 38 days to New York, making them truly fast ships on the Pacific. Each ship can carry 18 to 20 passengers, with extremely comfortable and perfect facilities, and especially exquisite cuisine, as the Danes are known for their culinary skills, even surpassing French cuisine. The cargo holds also have special equipment, making them ideal for transporting silk and bulk oil.
